<Review>Welp i really love this location because it is right around the corner of my house.

PARKING

I have to admit this is one of the worst parking lot. There are too much retail shops nearby and parking isn't just enough. I have tried finding parking for over 15 mins before, they are always jam busy packed in this parking lot. I dislike this! There are additional parking behind the building and yes there are usually one or 2 slots open. i would recommend you just jog or run or walk or bike if you live nearby. Otherwise be prepare to stress over parking

INTERIOR

Inside is alway busy. I think the slowest time is usually is the mid afternoon like one ish to 3 ish. Also inside is crowded with lots of machines in the cardio and weight room as well. Also sometimes really warm and smell of sweat is what you can smell.

MACHINES

They did have old cardio machines but lately they did some upgrade and got some new machines so this boosts the place for a additional star. They are usually wet and dirty after someones workout who don't wipe after themselves like todays treadmill i got on. I usually try not to touch the machines and if i do i will go wash hands asap.

WEIGHT ROOM

They are a bit more organized for the weights re racking. Sometimes it could be messy and in the wrong category while people mis re rack them. The weight room is small and i feel like everyone is looking at each other lol.

STAFFS

The employees here are usually friendly and helpful. They are nice and always greet you when you walk in or walk out. They help change channels or help you operate a machine if help is needed.

VIBE

The vibe in here i feel like its chill place. Also feel like i workout with lots of elder people since this gym is more elder people attend during day time. Sometimes i feel like the elders are way more healthy and in shape for me by always going and seeing them go at it lol. i feel like everyone who goes here are to workout and stay healthy and are friendly.

LOCKERS

The lockers are old and usually you will need to bring your own lock to lock your stuff. Also they have an open shower room with no privacy. The stalls are usually wet and humid from the steam from the shower rooms.

SAUANA AND STEAM ROOM AND JACUZZI

Love the steam room, i feel like i demo everything from my body after a good steam after my workout. It also relaxes all my muscles and aches and pains from the body. Also feels like i did a deep cleanse on my face like a facial dextox. It is wet inside and adding your sweat can make you drench when you walk out.

The sauna is a dry version of a steam room. This one is more popular than the steam room, because no one wants to be drenched wet and go into the car or back into the gym. Also i feel like this helps you dry off from the steam room. also love how you go in dry and come out with real sweat dripping from your face.

TO SUM IT UP

I love the location which is in a nice area. I also love how it is close to my home. Love how My goal of coming here to get a good quality workout and be done with my workout asap and get out of there. Also love how there is a starbucks like 2 min walk and get a ice cold drink after. Thanks for reading and have a good workout and day lol.</Review><Resp>None</Resp>< name>

< Review>
The Good: Most of staff are very nice / helpful -- Pocket facility is the closest 24-Hour gym to my house

The Bad: Old facility - ofter stifling (staff have to prop doors open) - bad odor - old equipment - a great number of exercise machines (e.g. elipticals, treadmils) are repeatedly broken and out of service for extended times - small and mostly overcrowded - unclean - people sneeze, cough, spit, sweat and bleed on mchines and only rarely do they even wipe the machines down when done - staff use to go through just about hourly wiping down and sanitizing machines, but haven't done that in several years now

Bottom Line: This 24-Hour facility has slid onto the bottom tier - I (and a large number of other current members) are looking forward to checking out the new California Family Fitnes Center (A Sacramento owned and operated company since 1991) opening in the Pocket area soon

NOTE: Be very leery of the 5-star rating someone gave to this facility 3 years ago -- it just doesn't jive with reality< /Review>

Me and my wife visited California in the spring of 2008. We were at L.A. during the Easter weekend. My wife is a 7th day Adventist. We decided to attend the Sabbath school and the worship the Saturday just before Easter Sunday at the iconic Hollywood Seven Day Adventist Church.
We arrived really early because of our 8hour jet lag. I remember the deep blue sky and the tall imperial palm trees on the street nearby. The church was not very crowded but we got a warm welcome.
I was impressed with the type of discussions the members had at the Sabbath School.
But what I really liked was the warm and cosy worship, the informality of the pastor and the impressive band (with guitar, bass, drums and keyboards). It was a very unconventional ceremony for our experiences but I still remember it as a memorable one.
Next time we visit LA I will try to go there again.
Cheers<//Text>

<rating>4<//rating>< text>
‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è‚≠êÔ∏è 1/2

Overall: This is one the more progressive Adventist churches I've attended. The church gives a breath of fresh air to those looking for a Christianity that addresses issues that many churches do not, yet does so in a welcoming, supportive, and positive way. If you're looking for great contemporary worship music, this is definitely a place to check out!  Hollywood has a great community with church members that welcome everyone, despite their background!

Welcomeness: When I entered the church, I was kindly greeted by someone with a smile and given a bulletin. The congregation was also warm and welcoming!

Environment (what it looked like)
The sanctuary was set up like an open auditorium with cushioned pews. It was well lit with natural lighting. There were many screens for lyrics and announcements which made it great to view from all seating angles.  The church's audio and visual system provided great sound and helpful slides which were projected to help the congregation follow along with the songs and the message. The lobby had a cafe feel with tables and chairs.

Atmosphere in church (the shared feelings from the building)
The church gives a meditative and comfortable atmosphere. The church was 30% filled which made you feel like you had a good deal of space to yourself.

Worship Music
The worship music, consisting of a full band with guitar, bass, keyboard, drums, and a few vocalists were great! Musicians were well polished and the vocalists sounded great together. There were four contemporary songs in the set that the congregation was very familiar with and participated at a high level.
- category: contemporary
- instrumentation type: guitar, bass, keyboard, drums, 3 vox
- quality:  great
- crowd engagement: high
- duration: 4 songs

Sermon
The head pastor preached a message that connected with the audience. His message was very contemporary, drawing metaphors and connections from today's events and culture. He had a story-telling delivery drawing stories from his life.  Rather than exclusive, his message was welcoming and inclusive to all people, all denominations, and all faiths. The sermon was reflective and thought provoking.
- Duration: 11:40-12:05

Service (Order of service)
- Opening song
- Worship & praise music
- Welcome & Greet
- Offering / song

Demographics
- ages: young adult - young professionals - adult
- family oriented: few families
- attendance: 60-70
- single ethnicity / multiple: plethora of various nationalities including Caucasian, African-American, Pacific Island / Asian, etc
- dress / attire: casual - business casual

Potluck: provided< /text>

<review>In the continuing effort to locate, taste and report on the breakfast burritos of the county, I bring Dos Hermanos Breakfast burritos. What fun, A nice drive to San Miguel to test another burrito. The place is busy, I mean busy, 20 minutes for a burrito. There are locals, to go orders, soldiers from Camp Roberts, and us! Popular, or the best place in town.. Well that is for each individual to decide. I had the chili verde breakfast burrito and my son had the bacon burrito. We were both very pleased with the content, size, preparation and flavors. I will be returning and bringing friends, relatives and others to this place to test the menu further. The staff are working their tails off as they serve both the in house and to go orders and are oh so polite and pleasant as they work. I will be back. Thank you Dos Hermanos! And I love the murals and the colorful decor, both inside and out! If you are on the freeway, pull off and enjoy a burrito, or call in an order and enjoy it in the park just up the street, either way it is a good stop.< /review>< Time>

< Text>
We first discovered this restaurant while driving down to SoCal on our way to Arizona, a couple of years ago (our home is in the East Bay Area near SF). Wanting just a snack, I chose a couple of chili verde tacos. MMMMMM; my mouth came alive with the wonderful flavor! From that trip onward, we make sure to stop whenever possible (almost any trip down or back up the 101), to get our chili verde fix. The combo plate is especially satisfying, which includes high quality refried beans and Mexican rice, along with tortillas. I'm honestly not sure I've ever had better chili verde, which is one of my go-to Mexican favorites. I hear people talk about the tamales and burritos, too, which I'm sure I'll try at some point.< /Text>

< Text>
This spot in Coronado is the most relaxing spot ever. It it completely silent the only sound you hear is the waves crashing into the rocks with a soothing fizz. You could bring your family or partner here to just have a good talk or just enjoy the view and relax. There are benches for you to sit and stare right into the abyss of the ocean and just over the horizon is downtown. Very accessible with parking and almost never packed.<//Text>

<gmapID>0x80deacaddb8f0b7b:0x55d50f60e7e36130<//gmapID><rate>1<//rate>< review>
Please note that this is a very small park, and that fishing is not legal here. The rocks behind the houses on 1st Street are privately owned by the houses, which is why the rocks look different behind each house. We didn't notice that. A homeowner called the police on fishermen who went on the rocks and they were ticketed for trespassing and fishing without a license. One of the guys said he didn't have any identification with him, and that conversation didn't go well with the police and miraculously he found his ID. Bayview Park ends where the houses around it begin, please be aware of that. Also as I am typing this (June 26) Bayview Park is actually CLOSED and will be closed for the next few weeks--- Not due to Corona but due to a sewer repair that required a complete excavation.<//review>

<text>I received a HSG two months ago, from another location and it was a horrific experience. It was the most excruciating pain ever and I was told both fallopian tubes were blocked, and that I was infertile. I am healthy, mid thirties, never had a painful menses, and have not had any underlying conditions that made sense for me to have these blockages so my Dr wanted a second opinion. She referred me to Dr. Chin assuring me that technique matters and that he is one of the best. I was extremely hesitant when I arrived because of my previous experience. Hazel, Dr. Chin's tech, greeted me and showed me where to change, she provided clear and accurate instructions with a warm and reassuring approach. Next, Dr. Chin welcomed my husband into the room to address any questions prior to the procedure. Hazel and Dr. Chin talked me through everything, went slowly, and performed the procedure methodically and seemingly painlessly! Hazel held my hand and reminded me to breathe throughout the procedure. I experienced mild cramping however, it was brief and tolerable. Dr. Chin has a refined approach that truly makes a difference! And while I appreciate him making the experience so much more tolerable, he also diacovered that both fallopian tubes are actually open!
